  FROM debian:bookworm
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      wget \
      git \
      openssl \
      libssl-dev \
      perl \
      sqlite3 \
      libsqlite3-dev \
      clang \
      dpkg \
      bash \
      coreutils \
      less \
      build-essential \
      pkg-config \
      cmake \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Homebrew/install/HEAD/install.sh && \
      bash install.sh && \
      rm install.sh && \
      echo 'eval "$(/home/linuxbrew/.linuxbrew/bin/brew shellenv)"' >> /root/.bashrc && \
      eval "$(/home/linuxbrew/.linuxbrew/bin/brew shellenv)"
  ENV PATH="/home/linuxbrew/.linuxbrew/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain 1.87.0
  ENV PATH="/root/.cargo/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN cargo install --version 0.106.2 nushell \
      && cargo install typos-cli \
      && cargo install carapace \
      && cargo install cross \
      && cargo install nu-highlight
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.config/nushell && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_config.nu /root/.config/nushell/config.nu
  RUN cargo build --release && \
      cargo test --workspace && \
      ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \
      ./scripts/install-all.sh
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:bookworm
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      wget \
      git \
      openssl \
      libssl-dev \
      perl \
      sqlite3 \
      libsqlite3-dev \
      clang \
      dpkg \
      bash \
      coreutils \
      less \
      build-essential \
      pkg-config \
      cmake \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain 1.87.0
  ENV PATH="/root/.cargo/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN cargo install --version 0.106.2 nushell \
      && cargo install typos-cli \
      && cargo install carapace \
      && cargo install cross \
      && cargo install nu-highlight
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.config/nushell && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_config.nu /root/.config/nushell/config.nu
  RUN cargo build --release && \
      cargo test --workspace && \
      ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \
      ./scripts/install-all.sh
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:bookworm
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      wget \
      git \
      openssl \
      libssl-dev \
      perl \
      sqlite3 \
      libsqlite3-dev \
      clang \
      dpkg \
      bash \
      coreutils \
      less \
      build-essential \
      pkg-config \
      cmake \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV PATH=$CARGO_HOME/bin:$PATH
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain stable
  RUN chmod -R a+w $CARGO_HOME
  RUN rustc --version && cargo --version
  RUN cargo install --version 0.106.2 nushell
  RUN cargo install typos-cli
  RUN cargo install carapace
  RUN cargo install cross
  RUN cargo install nu-highlight
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.config/nushell && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_config.nu /root/.config/nushell/config.nu
  RUN cargo build --release
  RUN cargo test --workspace
  RUN ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh
  RUN ./scripts/install-all.sh
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      pkg-config \
      cmake \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV PATH=$CARGO_HOME/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget https://sh.rustup.rs -O rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod +x rustup-init.sh && \
      ./rustup-init.sh -y --default-toolchain stable && \
      rm rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod -R a+w $CARGO_HOME
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      rustc --version && \
      cargo --version
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install --version 0.106.2 nushell && \
      cargo install typos-cli && \
      cargo install carapace && \
      cargo install cross && \
      cargo install nu-highlight
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.config/nushell && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_config.nu /root/.config/nushell/config.nu
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release && \
      cargo test --workspace && \
      ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \
      ./scripts/install-all.sh
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 7 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:bookworm
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      wget \
      git \
      openssl \
      libssl-dev \
      perl \
      sqlite3 \
      libsqlite3-dev \
      clang \
      dpkg \
      bash \
      coreutils \
      less \
      build-essential \
      pkg-config \
      cmake \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV PATH=$CARGO_HOME/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget https://sh.rustup.rs -O rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod +x rustup-init.sh && \
      ./rustup-init.sh -y --default-toolchain stable && \
      rm rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod -R a+w $CARGO_HOME
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      rustc --version && \
      cargo --version
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install --version 0.106.2 nushell && \
      cargo install typos-cli && \
      cargo install carapace && \
      cargo install cross && \
      cargo install nu-highlight
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.config/nushell && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_config.nu /root/.config/nushell/config.nu
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo test --workspace
  RUN chmod +x ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \
      chmod +x ./scripts/install-all.sh && \
      ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \
      ./scripts/install-all.sh
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:bookworm
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      wget \
      git \
      openssl \
      libssl-dev \
      perl \
      sqlite3 \
      libsqlite3-dev \
      clang \
      dpkg \
      bash \
      coreutils \
      less \
      build-essential \
      pkg-config \
      cmake \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV PATH=$CARGO_HOME/bin:$PATH
  RUN wget https://sh.rustup.rs -O rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod +x rustup-init.sh && \
      ./rustup-init.sh -y --default-toolchain stable && \
      rm rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod -R a+w $CARGO_HOME
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      rustc --version && \
      cargo --version
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install --locked --version 0.106.2 nushell
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install --locked typos-cli
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install --locked carapace
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install --locked cross
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install --locked nu-highlight
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.config/nushell && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_config.nu /root/.config/nushell/config.nu
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --locked
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo test --workspace --locked
  RUN chmod +x ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \
      chmod +x ./scripts/install-all.sh && \
      ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \
      ./scripts/install-all.sh
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \

      cargo build --release --locked
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo test --workspace --locked
  RUN chmod +x ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \

      ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \
      ./scripts/install-all.sh
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      wget \
      git \
      openssl \
      libssl-dev \
      perl \
      sqlite3 \
      libsqlite3-dev \
      clang \
      dpkg \
      bash \
      coreutils \
      less \
      build-essential \
      pkg-config \
      cmake \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV PATH=$CARGO_HOME/bin:$PATH
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.87.0
  RUN wget https://sh.rustup.rs -O rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod +x rustup-init.sh && \
      ./rustup-init.sh -y --default-toolchain $RUST_VERSION && \
      rm rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod -R a+w $CARGO_HOME
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      rustc --version && \
      cargo --version
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.config/nushell && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_config.nu /root/.config/nushell/config.nu
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --locked
  RUN chmod +x ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \
      chmod +x ./scripts/install-all.sh && \
      ./scripts/build-all-linux.sh && \
      ./scripts/install-all.sh
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV PATH=$CARGO_HOME/bin:$PATH
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.87.0
  RUN wget https://sh.rustup.rs -O rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod +x rustup-init.sh && \
      ./rustup-init.sh -y --default-toolchain $RUST_VERSION && \
      rm rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod -R a+w $CARGO_HOME
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      rustc --version && \
      cargo --version
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.config/nushell && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_config.nu /root/.config/nushell/config.nu
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --locked
  RUN chmod +x ./scripts/build-all.nu && \
      chmod +x ./scripts/install-all.sh && \
      ./scripts/build-all.nu && \
      ./scripts/install-all.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV PATH=$CARGO_HOME/bin:$PATH
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.87.0
  RUN wget https://sh.rustup.rs -O rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod +x rustup-init.sh && \
      ./rustup-init.sh -y --default-toolchain $RUST_VERSION && \
      rm rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod -R a+w $CARGO_HOME
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      rustc --version && \
      cargo --version
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.config/nushell && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_config.nu /root/.config/nushell/config.nu
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --locked
  RUN if [ -f "./scripts/build-all.nu" ]; then \
          chmod +x ./scripts/build-all.nu && \
          ./scripts/build-all.nu; \
      fi && \
      if [ -f "./scripts/install-all.sh" ]; then \
          chmod +x ./scripts/install-all.sh && \
          ./scripts/install-all.sh; \
      fi
  WORKDIR /workspace
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      wget \
      git \
      openssl \
      libssl-dev \
      perl \
      sqlite3 \
      libsqlite3-dev \
      clang \
      dpkg \
      bash \
      coreutils \
      less \
      build-essential \
      pkg-config \
      cmake \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV PATH=$CARGO_HOME/bin:$PATH
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.87.0
  RUN wget https://sh.rustup.rs -O rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod +x rustup-init.sh && \
      ./rustup-init.sh -y --default-toolchain $RUST_VERSION && \
      rm rustup-init.sh && \
      chmod -R a+w $CARGO_HOME
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      rustc --version && \
      cargo --version
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.config/nushell && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_env.nu /root/.config/nushell/env.nu && \
      cp crates/nu-utils/src/default_files/default_config.nu /root/.config/nushell/config.nu
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --locked
  WORKDIR /workspace
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
